*Grade 1 Maths — July Quiz*
_2842 questions (2342 new + 500 revision)_

*Q1.* 🎈 Arjun had 15 grapes but 4 flew away. How many grapes left?
A) 12
B) 10
C) 15
D) 11
✅ *Answer:* D) 11
💡 15 - 4 = 11 grapes left.

B) -
C) ×
D) +
✅ *Answer:* B) -
💡 The minus sign (-) means take away.

A) 45
B) 27
C) 26
D) 19
✅ *Answer:* C) 26
💡 Sorted: 19, 26, 45; middle is 26.
